 vijay ne 11 gendon par aath ran banaae
 Plessis became the victim of Rahul Sharma on the first ball of the tenth over
 sharma kii gend par vah wicketiper robin uthppa dwaara stump out kiye gaye
 At that time the team's score was 67 runs
 unhone 33 gendon par 43 ranon kii pari kheli
 Plessis hit five fours and two sixes
 iske baad chennai ne 12wein over main 86 ke kul yoga par suresh raina kaa wicket ganvaaya
 Raina scored 20 runs off 19 balls with the help of two fours
 vah sharma kii gend par steven smith dwaara lapke gaye
 Jadeja, who came to bat after Raina's dismissal, led the innings with captain Dhoni
 donon ke bich chauthe wicket ke liye 45 gendon par 61 ranon kii saajhedaari hui
 Jadeja scored 44 runs off 26 balls with the help of four fours and two sixes, while Dhoni hit a four off 28 balls and scored 26 runs
 jadeja ashish nehra kii gend par steven smith ke haathon boundry line par lapke gaye to dhoni dinda kii gend par murali karthik ke haathon lapke gaye
 Albie Morkel returned unbeaten after scoring three and Dwayne Bravo five
 pune kii ore se rahul sharma ne sabase adhik do wicket jatke
 Ashok Dinda, Ashish Nehra and Mathews took one wicket each
 chennai ne pune warirs india team ke khilaaf toss jitkar pehle ballebaaji karne kaa faisla kiya tha
 The comments warirs ko pichley mukaable main kings ilevan punjab se saat wicket se shikast jhelni padi thi jabaki superkings ne apane pichley mukaable main royal chalangers bangalore ko romaanchak mukaable main paanch wicket se haraaya tha
 The Warriors have won three of the four matches so far, losing in one match, while the Superkings have won two of the five fours and lost three
 chah ank lekar warirs ank talika main pehle sthaan par pahunch gaya he jabaki chaar ank lekar superkings chathe sthaan par virajman he
 Under the fifth edition of the Indian Premier League (IPL), the Pune Warriors team achieved the target of 156 runs scored by the Super Kings in the league match played at Subrata Roy Sahara Stadium on Saturday at the loss of three wickets with four balls to spare
 
 pune team ne jesi rider ke 73 or steven smith kii dhuandhar 44 ranon kii pari kii badaulat 156 ran banaakar yah match jeet liya or ank talika main sheersh sthaan hasil kiya
 Ryder scored 73 runs in 56 balls with the help of seven fours and a six, while Smith scored 44 off just 22 balls with the help of four fours and three sixes
 donon ke bich chauthe wicket ke liye naabad 66 ranon kii saajhedaari hui
 Ryder was awarded Man of the Match for his brilliant and restrained innings
 warirs ne dhuandhar ballebaaj robin uthppa, captain saurav ganguli or marlan samuels ke wicket ganvaae
 Uthappa scored 10 runs off seven balls with the help of a six
 vah durbhagyapurna tareeke se ran out hokar pavilion laute
 Ganguly also returned to the pavilion after being run out
 unhone 16 ran banaae
 Samuels could only score eight runs off 15 balls
 uthppa ne rider ke saath pari kii shuruyaat kii thi
 Captain Ganguly sent him to start the innings and himself came to bat on the first number
 chennai kii ore se ekmaatr wicket yo mahesh ke khate main gaya
 He bowled Samuels while two Pune batsmen were run out
 isse pehle, ganguli kii anbhavi captaini kii badaulat pune team superkings ko nirdhaarit 20 overon main paanch wicket ke nuksaan par 155 ran par rokane main safal rahi
 It was the same Chennai team that won the target of 205 runs set by Royal Challengers Bangalore in their last match
 olerounder rabindra jadeja ne sarvaadhik 44 ranon kii pari kheli vahiin salaami ballebaaj phalf du plasis ne 43 ranon kaa yogadan diya

 phalf du plasis or murali vijay ne chennai kii pari kii shuruyaat kii

 uthppa ne saat gendon par ek chakke kii madad se 10 ran banaae

 samuels 15 gendon par aath ran hi bana sake
 Uthappa started the innings with Rider
 captain ganguli ne unhen pari kii shuruyaat karne bheja or khud pehle nambar par ballebaaji karne aae

 unhone samuels ko bold kiya jabaki pune ke do ballebaaj ran out hue
 Earlier, thanks to the experienced captaincy of Ganguly, the Pune team managed to stop the Super Kings for 155 runs at the loss of five wickets in the stipulated 20 overs
 yah vahi chennai kii team thi jisane apane pichley mukaable main royal chalangers bangalore kii ore se rakhe gaye 205 ranon ke lakshya ko hasil kar jeet darj kii thi
 All-rounder Ravindra Jadeja scored the highest 44 runs while opener Faf du Plessis contributed 43 runs
 captain mahendra singh dhoni ne 26 ran banaae
 Faf du Plessis and Murali Vijay opened the innings for Chennai
 donon ne pehle wicket ke liye 43 ran jode
 Chennai got the first blow from the first ball of the seventh over as Vijay
 angelo maithyuj kii gend par lambaa shot lagane ke chakkar main vah ashok dinda ke haathon lapke gaye
 Vijay scored eight runs off 11 balls
 plasis dasven over kii pehali gend par rahul sharma kaa shikaar bane
 He was stumped by wicketkeeper Robin Uthappa off Sharma
 us samay team kaa score 67 ran tha
 He scored 43 runs off 33 balls
 plasis ne paanch chauke va do chakke lagaae
 After this, Chennai lost the wicket of Suresh Raina for a total of 86 in the 12th over
 raina ne 19 gendon par do chaukon kii madad se 20 ran banaae
 He was caught by Steven Smith off Sharma
 raina ke out hone ke baad ballebaaji karne aae jadeja ne captain dhoni ke saath milakar pari ko aage badhaayaa
 The two shared a 61-run partnership from 45 balls for the fourth wicket
 jadeja ne 26 gendon par chaar chaukon va do chhakkon kii madad se 44 ran banaae vahiin dhauni ne 28 gendon par ek chaukaa lagaaya or 26 ran banaae
 Jadeja was caught by Ashish Nehra at the boundary line in the hands of Steven Smith, while Murali Karthik was caught by Dhoni Dinda
 albi morkal teen or dwen braavo paanch ran banaakar naabad laute
 Rahul Sharma took the most two wickets from Pune
 ashok dinda, ashish nehra or maithyuj ke khate main ek-ek wicket gaya
 Chennai won the toss and decided to bat first against the Pune Warriors India team
 tippaniyan The Warriors suffered a seven-wicket defeat to Kings XI Punjab in the previous match, while the Super Kings defeated Royal Challengers Bangalore by five wickets in their last match

 Many of you may have thought that in the new year you will buy a new mobile phone, but by now you must have also understood that buying a new phone nowadays is not an easy task
 khaas taur par, agar aap 'smartphone' kharidne kii soch rahe hai to sahi phone chunanaa bhi ek chunauti he
 There are so many options in every budget that it is difficult to decide what to buy
 andrid phone kii aajkal sabase zyada dhooma he, lekin showrooms main jaakar dekhen to saare phone lagbhag ek jaise dikhte hai
 Everybody's features are also same and every company says its phone is the best
 aise main, aap puri tarah prachaar main kiye ja rahe daavon or celsman kii salaah ke bharose vishwaas kar lete hai
 Buy the phone and later regret seeing the friend's phone that i wish i had bought the same thing
 to aaj ham aapaki is mushkil ko kuch aasaan banaate hai
 If you follow these tips to buy a new smartphone, then you will not have to regret it later
 sabase pehla sawaal ye aata he ki blueberi khariden, yphone khariden, nokia lumia yaa phir andrid phone

 isliye un fitures ke liye kabhi apana bajet ne bigadane den jinka istemaal aap nahin karenge

 paise bhi bachenge, kaam bhi behatar hoga or bydaree bhi khub chalegi
 If you do not have to take big prints by taking photos from mobile, then do not be crazy about megapixels

 sies- bada he to behatar hephone kitna bada ho is bare main sabaki pasand alag-alag hoti he, lekin aajkal bade phone kaa chalan he
 There is such a competition among companies to offer big screen phones that the difference between phones, phablets and tablets has disappeared
 aamtaur par 4
 Phones with screens larger than 7 inches are considered 'big phones or phablets'
 4 inch se 4
 Phones with 7 inch screens are of medium size, and those less than 4 inches in size are classified as 'small phones'
 tach-screen phone main, screen par hi aapako likhnaa he or vahiin dekhnaa he
 Therefore, a very small size is not good
 iske alaava, badi screen par padhanaa, tip karnaa, photo yaa video dekhnaa aasaan hoga
 But the phone should not be too big, which is difficult to handle, or difficult to hold with one hand
 '5 inch ke aasapaas' kii screen sies har hisaab se behatar hoti he

 Consider three things
 risolution pipiai ( PPI -pixels per Inch) or screen LCD he yaa AMOLED
 Without much ado on what they mean, you can directly understand that the higher the resolution and the PPI, the better
 ye donon cheez jis phone main jitani zyada hogi, uski screen utani saaf, chamakdaar, sundar or gahare rangon vaali dikhegi
 The resolution of the screen determines whether it is HD or not
 isi tarah agar LCD or AMOLED screen ke bich chunanaa ho to aankh moond kar AMOLED hi chune

 darasal, ye ek khaas tarah kaa glass he jo screen ke upar lagaaya jaataa he
